<div id="noteTA-b150b844" class="noteTA"><div class="noteTA-group"><div data-noteta-group-source="module" data-noteta-group="IT"></div><div data-noteta-group-source="module" data-noteta-group="People"></div><div data-noteta-group-source="module" data-noteta-group="地名"></div><div data-noteta-group-source="module" data-noteta-group="Math"></div></div><div class="noteTA-local"><div data-noteta-code="zh-tw:其他版本;zh-cn:变体;"></div><div data-noteta-code="zh-tw:衍伸;zh-cn:变种;"></div></div></div>
<figure typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Maquina.png" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3d/Maquina.png/300px-Maquina.png" decoding="async" width="300" height="167" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3d/Maquina.png/450px-Maquina.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3d/Maquina.png/600px-Maquina.png 2x" data-file-width="1800" data-file-height="1000" /></a><figcaption>图灵机的艺术表示</figcaption></figure>
<p><b>图灵机</b>（英语：<span lang="en">Turing machine</span>），又称<b>确定型图灵机</b>，是<a href="/wiki/%E8%8B%B1%E5%9B%BD" title="英国">英国</a><a href="/wiki/%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6%E5%AE%B6" title="数学家">数学家</a><a href="/wiki/%E8%89%BE%E4%BC%A6%C2%B7%E5%9B%BE%E7%81%B5" title="艾伦·图灵">艾伦·图灵</a>于1936年提出的一种将人的计算行为抽象化的<a href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6%E9%80%BB%E8%BE%91%E6%9C%BA&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="数学逻辑机（页面不存在）">数学逻辑机</a>，其更抽象的意义为一种<a href="/wiki/%E8%AE%A1%E7%AE%97%E6%A8%A1%E5%9E%8B" class="mw-redirect" title="计算模型">计算模型</a>，可以看作等价于任何有限逻辑数学过程的终极强大逻辑机器。
</p>
<meta property="mw:PageProp/toc" />
<h2><span id=".E5.9B.BE.E7.81.B5.E7.9A.84.E5.9F.BA.E6.9C.AC.E6.80.9D.E6.83.B3"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="图灵的基本思想">图灵的基本思想</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9B%BE%E7%81%B5%E6%9C%BA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="编辑章节：图灵的基本思想"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>图灵的基本思想是用机器来模拟人们用纸笔进行<a href="/wiki/%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6" title="数学">数学</a>运算的过程，他把这样的过程看作下列两种简单的动作：
</p>
<ul><li>在纸上写上或擦除某个符号；</li>
<li>把注意力从纸的一处移动到另一处；</li></ul>
<p>而在每个阶段，人要决定下一步的动作，依赖于（a）此人当前所关注的纸上某个位置的符号和（b）此人当前思维的状态。
</p>
<figure typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Turing_machine_2a.svg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Turing_machine_2a.svg/300px-Turing_machine_2a.svg.png" decoding="async" width="300" height="55" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Turing_machine_2a.svg/450px-Turing_machine_2a.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Turing_machine_2a.svg/600px-Turing_machine_2a.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="550" data-file-height="100" /></a><figcaption>在某些模型中，纸带移动，而未用到的纸带真正是“空白”的。要进行的指令（<code>q4</code>）展示在扫描到方格之上（由Kleene（1952）p.375绘制）。</figcaption></figure>
<figure typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Turing_machine_2b.svg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/Turing_machine_2b.svg/300px-Turing_machine_2b.svg.png" decoding="async" width="300" height="71" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/Turing_machine_2b.svg/450px-Turing_machine_2b.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/Turing_machine_2b.svg/600px-Turing_machine_2b.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="550" data-file-height="130" /></a><figcaption>在某些模型中，读写头沿着固定的纸带移动。要进行的指令（<code>q1</code>）展示在读写头内。在这种模型中“空白”的纸带是全部为0的。有阴影的方格，包括读写头扫描到的空白，标记了1,1,B的那些方格，和读写头符号，构成了系统状态。（由Minsky（1967）p.121绘制）</figcaption></figure>
<p>为了模拟人的这种运算过程，图灵构造出一台假想的机器，该机器由以下几个部分组成：
</p>
<ol><li>一条无限长的纸带<b>TAPE</b>。纸带被划分为一个接一个的小格子，每个格子上包含一个来自有限字母表的符号，字母表中有一个特殊的符号<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \square }">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>&#x25FB;<!-- ◻ --></mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \square }</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/455831d58fa08f311b934d324adcff89a868b4e4" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.808ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle \square }"></span>表示空白。纸带上的格子从左到右依次被编号为0, 1, 2, ...，纸带的右端可以无限伸展。</li>
<li>一个读写头<b>HEAD</b>。它可以在纸带上左右移动，能读出当前所指的格子上的符号，并能改变它。</li>
<li>一套控制规则数量有限的<b>TABLE</b>（A finite table of instructions）。它根据当前机器所处的状态以及当前读写头所指的格子上的符号来确定读写头下一步的动作，并改变状态寄存器的值，令机器进入一个新的状态。<br />按照以下顺序告知图灵机命令：
<ul><li>1. 写入（替换）或擦除当前符号；</li>
<li>2. 移动 <b>HEAD</b>， 'L'向左， 'R'向右或者'N'不移动；</li>
<li>3. 保持当前状态或者转到另一状态。</li></ul></li>
<li>一个<b>状态寄存器</b>。它用来保存图灵机当前所处的状态。图灵机的所有可能状态的数目是有限的，并且有一个特殊的状态，称为<i>停机状态</i>。参见<a href="/wiki/%E5%81%9C%E6%9C%BA%E9%97%AE%E9%A2%98" title="停机问题">停机问题</a>。</li></ol>
<p>注意这个机器的每一部分都是有限的，但它有一个潜在的无限长的纸带，因此这种机器只是一个理想的设备。图灵认为这样的一台机器就能模拟人类所能进行的任何计算过程。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.9B.BE.E7.81.B5.E6.9C.BA.E7.9A.84.E6.AD.A3.E5.BC.8F.E5.AE.9A.E4.B9.89"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="图灵机的正式定义">图灵机的正式定义</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9B%BE%E7%81%B5%E6%9C%BA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="编辑章节：图灵机的正式定义"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>一台<b>图灵机</b>是一个七元有序组<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle (Q,\Sigma ,\Gamma ,\delta ,q_{0},q_{accept},q_{reject})}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>Q</mi>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <mi mathvariant="normal">&#x03A3;<!-- Σ --></mi>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <mi mathvariant="normal">&#x0393;<!-- Γ --></mi>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <mi>&#x03B4;<!-- δ --></mi>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <msub>
          <mi>q</mi>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mn>0</mn>
          </mrow>
        </msub>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <msub>
          <mi>q</mi>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mi>a</mi>
            <mi>c</mi>
            <mi>c</mi>
            <mi>e</mi>
            <mi>p</mi>
            <mi>t</mi>
          </mrow>
        </msub>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <msub>
          <mi>q</mi>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mi>r</mi>
            <mi>e</mi>
            <mi>j</mi>
            <mi>e</mi>
            <mi>c</mi>
            <mi>t</mi>
          </mrow>
        </msub>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle (Q,\Sigma ,\Gamma ,\delta ,q_{0},q_{accept},q_{reject})}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/65cd25157ac23bc91b8475d5738c8bff2fcbd575" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -1.005ex; width:27.398ex; height:3.009ex;" alt="{\displaystyle (Q,\Sigma ,\Gamma ,\delta ,q_{0},q_{accept},q_{reject})}"></span>，其中<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle Q,\Sigma ,\Gamma }">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>Q</mi>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <mi mathvariant="normal">&#x03A3;<!-- Σ --></mi>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <mi mathvariant="normal">&#x0393;<!-- Γ --></mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle Q,\Sigma ,\Gamma }</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/6f2e09e02847f0c4cf535504483e74ee4db5b5b7" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:7.037ex; height:2.509ex;" alt="{\displaystyle Q,\Sigma ,\Gamma }"></span>都是<a href="/wiki/%E6%9C%89%E9%99%90%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88" title="有限集合">有限集合</a>，且满足：
</p>
<ol><li><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle Q}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>Q</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle Q}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/8752c7023b4b3286800fe3238271bbca681219ed" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.838ex; height:2.509ex;" alt="{\displaystyle Q}"></span>是非空有穷状态集合；</li>
<li><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \Sigma }">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi mathvariant="normal">&#x03A3;<!-- Σ --></mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \Sigma }</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9e1f558f53cda207614abdf90162266c70bc5c1e" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.678ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle \Sigma }"></span>是非空有穷输入字母表，其中不包含特殊的空白符<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \square }">
  <semantics>

<li><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \Gamma }">

<li><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \delta :Q\times \Gamma \to Q\times \Gamma \times \{L,R,-\}}">

</p><p>开始的时候将输入符号串
<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \omega =\omega _{0}\omega _{1}\ldots \omega _{n-1}\in \Sigma ^{*}}">

从左到右依此填在纸带的第<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle 0,1,\ldots ,n-1}">

<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle M}">

<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle M}">

    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \delta }</annotation>

</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c5321cfa797202b3e1f8620663ff43c4660ea03a" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.049ex; height:2.343ex;" alt="{\displaystyle \delta }"></span>所描述的规则进行计算。例如，若当前机器的状态为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle q}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>q</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle q}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/06809d64fa7c817ffc7e323f85997f783dbdf71d" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.07ex; height:2.009ex;" alt="{\displaystyle q}"></span>，读写头所指的格子中的符号为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle x}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>x</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle x}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/87f9e315fd7e2ba406057a97300593c4802b53e4" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.33ex; height:1.676ex;" alt="{\displaystyle x}"></span>，设<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \delta (q,x)=(q',x',L)}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>&#x03B4;<!-- δ --></mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>q</mi>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <mi>x</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <msup>
          <mi>q</mi>
          <mo>&#x2032;</mo>
        </msup>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <msup>
          <mi>x</mi>
          <mo>&#x2032;</mo>
        </msup>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <mi>L</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \delta (q,x)=(q',x',L)}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/062b189bab7913ba27fb501fb330c47a56ad9a76" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:18.628ex; height:3.009ex;" alt="{\displaystyle \delta (q,x)=(q&#039;,x&#039;,L)}"></span>，则机器进入新状态<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle q'}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <msup>
          <mi>q</mi>
          <mo>&#x2032;</mo>
        </msup>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle q'}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/912405e5d416048908ea7978929975843d2ee4e6" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.764ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle q&#039;}"></span>，将读写头所指的格子中的符号改为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle x'}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <msup>
          <mi>x</mi>
          <mo>&#x2032;</mo>
        </msup>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle x'}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0ac74959896052e160a5953102e4bc3850fe93b2" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.014ex; height:2.509ex;" alt="{\displaystyle x&#039;}"></span>，然后将读写头向左移动一个格子。若在某一时刻，读写头所指的是第0号格子，但根据转移函数它下一步将继续向左移，这时它停在原地不动。换句话说，读写头始终不移出纸带的左边界。若在某个时刻<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle M}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>M</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle M}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f82cade9898ced02fdd08712e5f0c0151758a0dd" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.442ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle M}"></span>根据转移函数进入了状态<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle q_{accept}}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <msub>
          <mi>q</mi>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mi>a</mi>
            <mi>c</mi>
            <mi>c</mi>
            <mi>e</mi>
            <mi>p</mi>
            <mi>t</mi>
          </mrow>
        </msub>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle q_{accept}}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/abc876ac44dfafd4dab9e5b78a6b7fa69e574134" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -1.005ex; width:5.75ex; height:2.343ex;" alt="{\displaystyle q_{accept}}"></span>，则它立刻停机并接受输入的字符串；
若在某个时刻<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle M}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>M</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle M}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f82cade9898ced02fdd08712e5f0c0151758a0dd" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.442ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle M}"></span>根据转移函数进入了状态<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle q_{reject}}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <msub>
          <mi>q</mi>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mi>r</mi>
            <mi>e</mi>
            <mi>j</mi>
            <mi>e</mi>
            <mi>c</mi>
            <mi>t</mi>
          </mrow>
        </msub>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle q_{reject}}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ee3d04a3dd9d593430e937710b5ca63c8fe8b9bd" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -1.005ex; width:5.526ex; height:2.343ex;" alt="{\displaystyle q_{reject}}"></span>，则它立刻停机并拒绝输入的字符串。
</p><p>注意，转移函数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \delta }">

</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.9B.BE.E7.81.B5.E6.9C.BA.E7.9A.84.E5.9F.BA.E6.9C.AC.E6.9C.AF.E8.AF.AD"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="图灵机的基本术语">图灵机的基本术语</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9B%BE%E7%81%B5%E6%9C%BA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="编辑章节：图灵机的基本术语"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>设<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle M=(Q,\Sigma ,\Gamma ,\delta ,q_{0},q_{accept},q_{reject})}">

</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/48eff443f9de7a985bb94ca3bde20813ea737be8" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.446ex; height:1.676ex;" alt="{\displaystyle \omega }"></span>，且<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle C_{1},C_{2},\ldots ,C_{k}}">

          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

          </mrow>
        </msub>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle C_{1},C_{2},\ldots ,C_{k}}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2426e2e1053c32b204320ac08efb1e2baaeaa09d" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:14.395ex; height:2.509ex;" alt="{\displaystyle C_{1},C_{2},\ldots ,C_{k}}"></span>称为图灵机<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle M}">

  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>M</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>

  </semantics>

</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.9B.BE.E7.81.B5.E6.9C.BA.E7.9A.84.E4.BE.8B.E5.AD.90"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="图灵机的例子">图灵机的例子</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9B%BE%E7%81%B5%E6%9C%BA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="编辑章节：图灵机的例子"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>设<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle M=(\{0,1,10,11\},\{0,1\},\{0,1,\square \},\delta ,0,,)}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>M</mi>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mo fence="false" stretchy="false">{</mo>
        <mn>0</mn>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <mn>1</mn>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <mn>10</mn>
        <mo>,</mo>

        <mo fence="false" stretchy="false">}</mo>

        <mo fence="false" stretchy="false">{</mo>
        <mn>0</mn>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <mn>1</mn>
        <mo fence="false" stretchy="false">}</mo>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <mo fence="false" stretchy="false">{</mo>
        <mn>0</mn>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <mn>1</mn>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <mi>&#x25FB;<!-- ◻ --></mi>
        <mo fence="false" stretchy="false">}</mo>

    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle M=(\{0,1,10,11\},\{0,1\},\{0,1,\square \},\delta ,0,,)}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/fb406072dbf2ba888db9ad135f0fc6ec73e63736" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:42.376ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle M=(\{0,1,10,11\},\{0,1\},\{0,1,\square \},\delta ,0,,)}"></span>和<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \delta :\{0,1,10,11\}\times \{0,1\}\to \{0,1,10,11\}\times \{0,1\}\times \{R,L,E,S\}}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>&#x03B4;<!-- δ --></mi>
        <mo>:</mo>
        <mo fence="false" stretchy="false">{</mo>
        <mn>0</mn>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <mn>1</mn>

        <mn>10</mn>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <mn>11</mn>

        <mo>&#x00D7;<!-- × --></mo>
        <mo fence="false" stretchy="false">{</mo>
        <mn>0</mn>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <mn>1</mn>
        <mo fence="false" stretchy="false">}</mo>
        <mo stretchy="false">&#x2192;<!-- → --></mo>

        <mo>,</mo>
        <mn>1</mn>
        <mo fence="false" stretchy="false">}</mo>
        <mo>&#x00D7;<!-- × --></mo>
        <mo fence="false" stretchy="false">{</mo>
        <mi>R</mi>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <mi>L</mi>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <mi>E</mi>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <mi>S</mi>
        <mo fence="false" stretchy="false">}</mo>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \delta :\{0,1,10,11\}\times \{0,1\}\to \{0,1,10,11\}\times \{0,1\}\times \{R,L,E,S\}}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a6763d8abbf12ac3c166628ccbbb0878a18d403d" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:63.34ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle \delta :\{0,1,10,11\}\times \{0,1\}\to \{0,1,10,11\}\times \{0,1\}\times \{R,L,E,S\}}"></span>.
比如做一个以1的个数表示数值的加法运算，在磁带上的数据是0000001110110000，就是3+2的意思。程序<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \delta }">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>&#x03B4;<!-- δ --></mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \delta }</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c5321cfa797202b3e1f8620663ff43c4660ea03a" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.049ex; height:2.343ex;" alt="{\displaystyle \delta }"></span>如下：
</p>
<dl><dd>0,0 -&gt; 0,0R</dd>
<dd>0,1 -&gt; 1,1R</dd>
<dd>1,0 -&gt; 10,1R</dd>
<dd>1,1 -&gt; 1,1R</dd>
<dd>10,0 -&gt; 11,0L</dd>
<dd>10,1 -&gt; 10,1R</dd>
<dd>11,0 -&gt; E</dd>
<dd>11,1 -&gt; 0,0S</dd></dl>
<p>第一行程序0,0-&gt;0,0R意思就是如果机器读到0，就将其变成0，状态变为0，读写头向右移动一格. R就是向右移动一格，L就是向左移一格，E是错误，S是停机. xx,y -&gt; aa,b中xx是当前状态, y是当前格子的值, aa是程序下一步的状态, b是当前格的修改值。
</p><p>虽然这里给出与上面不同形式的定义，但两者是等价的，这里的定义能完成的工作并不比上面的定义多。
</p>

<h2><span id=".E9.80.9A.E7.94.A8.E5.9B.BE.E7.81.B5.E6.9C.BA"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="通用图灵机">通用图灵机</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9B%BE%E7%81%B5%E6%9C%BA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="编辑章节：通用图灵机"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E9%80%9A%E7%94%A8%E5%9B%BE%E7%81%B5%E6%9C%BA" class="mw-redirect" title="通用图灵机">通用图灵机</a></div>
<p>对于任意一个图灵机，因为它的描述是有限的，因此我们总可以用某种方式将其编码为字符串。我们用<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \langle M\rangle }">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mo fence="false" stretchy="false">&#x27E8;<!-- ⟨ --></mo>
        <mi>M</mi>
        <mo fence="false" stretchy="false">&#x27E9;<!-- ⟩ --></mo>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \langle M\rangle }</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/39fd611a3aea4bb376f687b64d11c37ea7eeac53" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:4.251ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle \langle M\rangle }"></span>表示图灵机<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle M}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>M</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle M}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f82cade9898ced02fdd08712e5f0c0151758a0dd" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.442ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle M}"></span>的编码。
</p><p>我们可以构造出一个特殊的图灵机，它接受任意一个图灵机<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle M}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>M</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle M}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f82cade9898ced02fdd08712e5f0c0151758a0dd" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.442ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle M}"></span>的编码<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \langle M\rangle }">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mo fence="false" stretchy="false">&#x27E8;<!-- ⟨ --></mo>
        <mi>M</mi>
        <mo fence="false" stretchy="false">&#x27E9;<!-- ⟩ --></mo>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \langle M\rangle }</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/39fd611a3aea4bb376f687b64d11c37ea7eeac53" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:4.251ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle \langle M\rangle }"></span>，然后模拟图灵机<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle M}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>M</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle M}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f82cade9898ced02fdd08712e5f0c0151758a0dd" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.442ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle M}"></span>的运作，这样的图灵机称为<b>通用图灵机</b>（Universal Turing Machine）。现代电子计算机的计算模型其实就是这样一种通用图灵机，它先接受一段描述另一图灵机，例如图灵机<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle X}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>X</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle X}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/68baa052181f707c662844a465bfeeb135e82bab" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.98ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle X}"></span>的action table的字符串，然后运行写给图灵机<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle X}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>X</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle X}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/68baa052181f707c662844a465bfeeb135e82bab" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.98ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle X}"></span>的程序<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle Y}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>Y</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle Y}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/961d67d6b454b4df2301ac571808a3538b3a6d3f" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.171ex; width:1.773ex; height:2.009ex;" alt="{\displaystyle Y}"></span>，这样通用图灵机执行程序<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle Y}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>Y</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle Y}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/961d67d6b454b4df2301ac571808a3538b3a6d3f" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.171ex; width:1.773ex; height:2.009ex;" alt="{\displaystyle Y}"></span>就像图灵机<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle X}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>X</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle X}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/68baa052181f707c662844a465bfeeb135e82bab" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.98ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle X}"></span>一样，能正确执行并实现程序<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle Y}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>Y</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle Y}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/961d67d6b454b4df2301ac571808a3538b3a6d3f" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.171ex; width:1.773ex; height:2.009ex;" alt="{\displaystyle Y}"></span>所描述的算法。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.9B.BE.E7.81.B5.E6.9C.BA.E7.9A.84.E5.8F.98.E4.BD.93"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="图灵机的变体">图灵机的变体</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9B%BE%E7%81%B5%E6%9C%BA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="编辑章节：图灵机的变体"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>图灵机有很多变种，但可以证明这些变种的计算能力都是等价的，即它们识别同样的语言类。证明两个计算模型<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle A}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>A</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7daff47fa58cdfd29dc333def748ff5fa4c923e3" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.743ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle A}"></span>和<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle B}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>B</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle B}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/47136aad860d145f75f3eed3022df827cee94d7a" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.764ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle B}"></span>的计算能力等价的基本思想是：用<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle A}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>A</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7daff47fa58cdfd29dc333def748ff5fa4c923e3" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.743ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle A}"></span>和<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle B}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>B</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle B}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/47136aad860d145f75f3eed3022df827cee94d7a" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.764ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle B}"></span>相互模拟，若<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle A}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>A</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7daff47fa58cdfd29dc333def748ff5fa4c923e3" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.743ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle A}"></span>可模拟<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle B}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>B</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle B}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/47136aad860d145f75f3eed3022df827cee94d7a" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.764ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle B}"></span>且<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle B}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>B</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle B}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/47136aad860d145f75f3eed3022df827cee94d7a" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.764ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle B}"></span>可模拟<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle A}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>A</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/7daff47fa58cdfd29dc333def748ff5fa4c923e3" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.743ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle A}"></span>，显然他们的计算能力等价。注意这里我们暂时不考虑计算的效率，只考虑计算的理论上“可行性”。
</p><p>首先我们可以发现，改变图灵机的带字母表并不会改变其计算能力。例如我们可以限制图灵机的带字母表为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \{0,1\}}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mo fence="false" stretchy="false">{</mo>
        <mn>0</mn>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <mn>1</mn>
        <mo fence="false" stretchy="false">}</mo>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \{0,1\}}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/28de5781698336d21c9c560fb1cbb3fb406923eb" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:5.684ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle \{0,1\}}"></span>，这并不会改变图灵机的计算能力，因为我们显然可以用带字母表为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \{0,1\}}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mo fence="false" stretchy="false">{</mo>
        <mn>0</mn>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <mn>1</mn>
        <mo fence="false" stretchy="false">}</mo>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \{0,1\}}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/28de5781698336d21c9c560fb1cbb3fb406923eb" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:5.684ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle \{0,1\}}"></span>的图灵机模拟带字母表为任意有限集合<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \Gamma }">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi mathvariant="normal">&#x0393;<!-- Γ --></mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \Gamma }</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4cfde86a3f7ec967af9955d0988592f0693d2b19" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.453ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle \Gamma }"></span>的图灵机。
</p><p>另一个要注意的是，如果我们允许图灵机的纸带两端都可以无限伸展，这并不能增加图灵机的计算能力，因为我们显然可以用只有纸带一端能无限伸展的图灵机来模拟这种纸带两端都可以无限伸展的图灵机。
</p><p>如果我们允许图灵机的读写头在某一步保持原地不动，那也不会增加其计算能力，因为我们可以用向左移动一次再向右移动一次来代替在原地不动。
</p><p>其它的常见图灵机变种包括：
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/%E5%A4%9A%E5%B8%A6%E5%9B%BE%E7%81%B5%E6%9C%BA" title="多带图灵机">多带图灵机</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E9%9D%9E%E7%A1%AE%E5%AE%9A%E5%9E%8B%E5%9B%BE%E7%81%B5%E6%9C%BA" title="非确定型图灵机">非确定型图灵机</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%A4%E6%9B%BF%E5%BC%8F%E5%9B%BE%E7%81%B5%E6%9C%BA" title="交替式图灵机">交替式图灵机</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E6%9E%9A%E4%B8%BE%E5%99%A8" title="枚举器">枚举器</a></li></ul>
<h2><span id=".E5.9B.BE.E7.81.B5.E5.8F.AF.E8.AE.A1.E7.AE.97.E6.80.A7"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="图灵可计算性">图灵可计算性</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9B%BE%E7%81%B5%E6%9C%BA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="编辑章节：图灵可计算性"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/%E5%9B%BE%E7%81%B5%E5%8F%AF%E8%AF%86%E5%88%AB%E8%AF%AD%E8%A8%80" class="mw-redirect" title="图灵可识别语言">图灵可识别语言</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E5%9B%BE%E7%81%B5%E5%8F%AF%E5%88%A4%E5%AE%9A%E8%AF%AD%E8%A8%80" class="mw-redirect" title="图灵可判定语言">图灵可判定语言</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E9%80%92%E5%BD%92%E5%8F%AF%E6%9E%9A%E4%B8%BE%E8%AF%AD%E8%A8%80" title="递归可枚举语言">递归可枚举语言</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%AF%E8%AE%A1%E7%AE%97%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="可计算函数">可计算函数</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E9%80%92%E5%BD%92%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="递归函数">递归函数</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E5%81%9C%E6%9C%BA%E9%97%AE%E9%A2%98" title="停机问题">停机问题</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%AF%E5%88%A4%E5%AE%9A%E6%80%A7" title="可判定性">可判定性</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%8D%E5%8F%AF%E5%88%A4%E5%AE%9A%E6%80%A7" class="mw-redirect" title="不可判定性">不可判定性</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%8D%E5%8F%AF%E8%A7%A3%E5%BA%A6" title="不可解度">不可解度</a></li></ul>
<h2><span id=".E5.85.B6.E5.AE.83.E7.AD.89.E4.BB.B7.E7.9A.84.E8.AE.A1.E7.AE.97.E6.A8.A1.E5.9E.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="其它等价的计算模型">其它等价的计算模型</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9B%BE%E7%81%B5%E6%9C%BA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="编辑章节：其它等价的计算模型"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>除了图灵机以外，人们还发明了很多其它的<a href="/wiki/%E8%AE%A1%E7%AE%97%E6%A8%A1%E5%9E%8B_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)" title="计算模型 (数学)">计算模型</a>。包括：
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/%E5%AF%84%E5%AD%98%E5%99%A8%E6%9C%BA" title="寄存器机">寄存器机</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E9%80%92%E5%BD%92%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0" title="递归函数">递归函数</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%CE%9B%E6%BC%94%E7%AE%97" title="Λ演算">λ演算</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E7%94%9F%E5%91%BD%E6%B8%B8%E6%88%8F" class="mw-redirect" title="生命游戏">生命游戏</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E9%A9%AC%E5%B0%94%E5%8F%AF%E5%A4%AB%E7%AE%97%E6%B3%95" title="马尔可夫算法">马尔可夫算法</a></li></ul>
<p>然而这些模型无一例外地都和图灵机的计算能力等价，因此<a href="/wiki/%E9%82%B1%E5%A5%87" class="mw-redirect" title="邱奇">邱奇</a>，<a href="/wiki/%E5%9B%BE%E7%81%B5" class="mw-redirect" title="图灵">图灵</a>和<a href="/wiki/%E5%93%A5%E5%BE%B7%E5%B0%94" class="mw-redirect" title="哥德尔">哥德尔</a>
提出了著名的<a href="/wiki/%E9%82%B1%E5%A5%87-%E5%9B%BE%E7%81%B5%E8%AE%BA%E9%A2%98" title="邱奇-图灵论题">邱奇-图灵论题</a>：一切<i>直觉上能计算</i>的函数都可用图灵机计算，反之亦然。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.AE.9A.E7.90.86"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="定理">定理</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9B%BE%E7%81%B5%E6%9C%BA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="编辑章节：定理"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/%E5%85%8B%E8%8E%B1%E5%B0%BC%E2%80%93%E6%B3%A2%E6%96%AF%E7%89%B9%E5%AE%9A%E7%90%86" title="克莱尼–波斯特定理">克莱尼–波斯特定理</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E5%BC%97%E9%87%8C%E5%BE%B7%E5%A0%A1%E2%80%93%E7%A9%86%E5%A5%87%E5%B0%BC%E5%85%8B%E5%AE%9A%E7%90%86" title="弗里德堡–穆奇尼克定理">弗里德堡–穆奇尼克定理</a></li>

<h2><span id=".E5.8F.82.E8.80.83.E6.96.87.E7.8C.AE"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="参考文献">参考文献</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9B%BE%E7%81%B5%E6%9C%BA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="编辑章节：参考文献"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Turing, A., <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.abelard.org/turpap2/tp2-ie.asp">On Computable Numbers, With an Application to the Entscheidungsproblem</a>（<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="//web.archive.org/web/20040403210049/http://www.abelard.org/turpap2/tp2-ie.asp">页面存档备份</a>，存于<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%92%E8%81%94%E7%BD%91%E6%A1%A3%E6%A1%88%E9%A6%86" title="互联网档案馆">互联网档案馆</a>）, Proceedings of the London Mathematical Society, Series 2, Volume 42, 1936; reprinted in M. David（ed.）, The Undecidable, Hewlett, NY: Raven Press, 1965;</li>
<li>Michael Sipser,  Introduction to the Theory of Computation, PWS Publishing, 1997. <a href="/wiki/Special:%E7%BD%91%E7%BB%9C%E4%B9%A6%E6%BA%90/053494728X" class="internal mw-magiclink-isbn">ISBN 0-534-94728-X</a></li></ul>
<h2><span id=".E5.A4.96.E9.83.A8.E9.93.BE.E6.8E.A5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="外部链接">外部链接</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%9B%BE%E7%81%B5%E6%9C%BA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="编辑章节：外部链接"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.cheransoft.com/vturing/">Visual Turing, a Turing machine interactive simulator/IDE</a>（<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="//web.archive.org/web/20040407193325/http://www.cheransoft.com/vturing/">页面存档备份</a>，存于<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%92%E8%81%94%E7%BD%91%E6%A1%A3%E6%A1%88%E9%A6%86" title="互联网档案馆">互联网档案馆</a>）（free software for Windows）。</li>
